\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01449}01449 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01450}01450 \textcolor{comment}{//                               Hashing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01451}01451 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01452}01452 \textcolor{comment}{//      typical use for this is to make a power-\/of-\/two hash table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01453}01453 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01454}01454 \textcolor{comment}{//      let N = size of table (2\string^n)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01455}01455 \textcolor{comment}{//      let H = stb\_hash(str)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01456}01456 \textcolor{comment}{//      let S = stb\_rehash(H) | 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01457}01457 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01458}01458 \textcolor{comment}{//      then hash probe sequence P(i) for i=0..N-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01459}01459 \textcolor{comment}{//         P(i) = (H + S*i) \& (N-\/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01460}01460 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01461}01461 \textcolor{comment}{//      the idea is that H has 32 bits of hash information, but the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01462}01462 \textcolor{comment}{//      table has only, say, 2\string^20 entries so only uses 20 of the bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01463}01463 \textcolor{comment}{//      then by rehashing the original H we get 2\string^12 different probe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01464}01464 \textcolor{comment}{//      sequences for a given initial probe location. (So it's optimal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01465}01465 \textcolor{comment}{//      for 64K tables and its optimality decreases past that.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01466}01466 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01467}01467 \textcolor{comment}{//      ok, so I've added something that generates \_two separate\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01468}01468 \textcolor{comment}{//      32-\/bit hashes simultaneously which should scale better to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01469}01469 \textcolor{comment}{//      very large tables.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01470}01470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01471}01471 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STB\_INCLUDE\_STB\_LIB\_H}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01617}01617 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01618}01618 \textcolor{comment}{// Hash table: call stb\_define\_hash(TYPE,N,KEY,K1,K2,HASH,VALUE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01619}01619 \textcolor{comment}{//     TYPE     -\/-\/ will define a structure type containing the hash table}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01622}01622 \textcolor{comment}{//                        N destroy}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01625}01625 \textcolor{comment}{//                        N remove}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01626}01626 \textcolor{comment}{//     KEY      -\/-\/ the type of the key. 'x == y' must be valid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01627}01627 \textcolor{comment}{//       K1,K2  -\/-\/ keys never used by the app, used as flags in the hashtable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01628}01628 \textcolor{comment}{//       HASH   -\/-\/ a piece of code ending with 'return' that hashes key 'k'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01629}01629 \textcolor{comment}{//     VALUE    -\/-\/ the type of the value. 'x = y' must be valid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01630}01630 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01631}01631 \textcolor{comment}{//  Note that stb\_define\_hash\_base can be used to define more sophisticated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l01632}01632 \textcolor{comment}{//  hash tables, e.g. those that make copies of the key or use special}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03136}03136             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} *candidate == 0 ? 0 : -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03137}03137          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*expr == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03138}03138             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!*candidate) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03139}03139          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03140}03140             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (insensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03141}03141                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tolower(*candidate) != tolower(*expr))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03142}03142                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03143}03143             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03144}03144                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*candidate != *expr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03145}03145                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03146}03146          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03147}03147          ++candidate, ++expr, ++where;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03148}03148       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03149}03149    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03150}03150       \textcolor{comment}{// 0-\/length search string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03151}03151       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!*expr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03152}03152          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03153}03153    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03154}03154 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03155}03155    assert(search || *expr == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03156}03156    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!search)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03157}03157       ++expr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03158}03158 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03159}03159    \textcolor{comment}{// implicit '*' at this point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03160}03160       }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03161}03161    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (*expr) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03162}03162       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} o=0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03163}03163       \textcolor{comment}{// combine redundant * characters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03164}03164       \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (expr[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) ++expr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03165}03165 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03166}03166       \textcolor{comment}{// ok, at this point, expr[-\/1] == '*',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03167}03167       \textcolor{comment}{// and expr[0] != '*'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03168}03168 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03169}03169       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!expr[0]) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} start >= 0 ? start : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03170}03170 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03171}03171       \textcolor{comment}{// now find next '*'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03172}03172       o = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03173}03173       \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (expr[o] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03174}03174          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (expr[o] == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03175}03175             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03176}03176          ++o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03177}03177       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03178}03178       \textcolor{comment}{// if no '*', scan to end, then match at end}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03179}03179       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (expr[o] == 0 \&\& !search) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03180}03180          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03181}03181          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (z=0; z < o; ++z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03182}03182             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (candidate[z] == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03183}03183                \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03184}03184          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (candidate[z])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03185}03185             ++z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03186}03186          \textcolor{comment}{// ok, now check if they match}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03187}03187          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stb\_\_match\_qstring(candidate+z-\/o, expr, o, insensitive))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03188}03188             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} start >= 0 ? start : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03189}03189          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1; }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03190}03190       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03191}03191          \textcolor{comment}{// if yes '*', then do stb\_\_find\_qmatch on the intervening chars}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03192}03192          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = stb\_\_find\_qstring(candidate, expr, o, insensitive);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03193}03193          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (n < 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03194}03194             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03195}03195          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (start < 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03196}03196             start = where + n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03197}03197          expr += o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03198}03198          candidate += n+o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03199}03199       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03200}03200 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03201}03201       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*expr == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03202}03202          assert(search);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03203}03203          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} start;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03204}03204       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03205}03205 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03206}03206       assert(*expr == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03207}03207       ++expr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03208}03208    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03209}03209 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03210}03210    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} start >= 0 ? start : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03211}03211 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03212}03212 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03213}03213 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stb\_\_wildmatch\_raw(\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *expr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *candidate, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} search, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} insensitive)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03214}03214 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03215}03215    \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} \mbox{\hyperlink{classbuffer}{buffer}}[256];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03216}03216    \textcolor{comment}{// handle multiple search strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03217}03217    \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *s = strchr(expr, \textcolor{charliteral}{';'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03218}03218    \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *last = expr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03219}03219    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (s) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03220}03220       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03221}03221       \textcolor{comment}{// need to allow for non-\/writeable strings... assume they're small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03222}03222       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s -\/ last < 256) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03223}03223          stb\_strncpy(\mbox{\hyperlink{classbuffer}{buffer}}, last, s-\/last+1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03224}03224          z = stb\_\_wildmatch\_raw2(\mbox{\hyperlink{classbuffer}{buffer}}, candidate, search, insensitive);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03225}03225       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03226}03226          *s = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03227}03227          z = stb\_\_wildmatch\_raw2(last, candidate, search, insensitive);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03228}03228          *s = \textcolor{charliteral}{';'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03229}03229       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03230}03230       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03231}03231       last = s+1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03232}03232       s = strchr(last, \textcolor{charliteral}{';'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03233}03233    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__lib_8h_source_l03234}03234    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stb\_\_wildmatch\_raw2(last, candidate, search, insensitive);}
